## Idea

Transpositions are permutations of two elements

## Properties

### `transposition` is not the identity equivalence

<pre class="Agda"><a id="7127" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="7134" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7134" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="7138" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7139" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7139" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="7142" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7142" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="7145" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7147" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="7152" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7154" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7155" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7155" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="7157" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7159" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="7162" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7139" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="7164" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7166" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7167" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7167" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="7169" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7171" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7155" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="7173" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7175" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#1873" class="Function">decidable-Prop</a> <a id="7190" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7142" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="7192" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="7196" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7197" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7197" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="7199" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7201" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4379" class="Function">has-cardinality</a> <a id="7217" class="Number">2</a> <a id="7219" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7220" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#502" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="7222" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7155" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="7224" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="7227" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7227" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7229" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7231" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#2131" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="7251" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7252" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7167" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="7254" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7227" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7255" class="Symbol">))))</a>

  <a id="7271" class="Keyword">abstract</a>

                    <a id="7890" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7892" href="foundation.function-extensionality.html#946" class="Function">htpy-eq</a> <a id="7900" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7398" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="7902" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7510" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7903" class="Symbol">))</a>
                  <a id="7924" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7926" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#2649" class="Function">eq-is-prop</a> <a id="7937" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7938" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#2228" class="Function">is-prop-type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="7966" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7967" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7167" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="7969" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#7510" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7970" class="Symbol">)))}))</a>
</pre>
### For any type `X` with decidable equality and `x y : X` such that `x` and `y` are distinct, there exists a transposition that maps `x` to `y`, `y` to `x` and everything else to itself.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="8179" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="8186" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8186" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="8190" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8191" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8191" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="8193" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8195" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="8200" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8202" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8203" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8203" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="8205" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8207" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="8210" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8191" class="Bound">l</a><a id="8211" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8213" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8214" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8214" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="8216" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8218" href="foundation.decidable-equality.html#1785" class="Function">has-decidable-equality</a> <a id="8241" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8203" class="Bound">X</a><a id="8242" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="8246" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="8414" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="8418" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8419" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="8423" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8424" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8255" class="Function">transposition-two-elements</a> <a id="8451" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8451" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8453" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8453" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8455" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8455" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8456" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8458" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8458" class="Bound">z</a><a id="8459" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8461" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8463" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1168" class="Datatype">coprod</a> <a id="8470" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8471" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#641" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="8474" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8451" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8476" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8458" class="Bound">z</a><a id="8477" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8479" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8480" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#641" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="8483" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8453" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8485" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8458" class="Bound">z</a><a id="8486" class="Symbol">)</a>

          <a id="17550" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#694" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="17555" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#694" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="17560" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#694" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="17564" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Transpositions can be transported along equivalences

<pre class="Agda"><a id="17637" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="17644" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17644" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="17648" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17649" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17649" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="17652" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17652" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="17655" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17655" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="17658" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17658" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="17661" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17663" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="17668" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17670" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17671" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17671" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="17673" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17675" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="17678" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17649" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="17680" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17682" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17683" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17683" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="17685" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17687" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="17690" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17652" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="17692" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17694" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17695" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17695" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="17697" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17699" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17671" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="17701" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="17703" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17683" class="Bound">Y</a><a id="17704" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="17708" class="Keyword">where</a>

        <a id="23505" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23507" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23509" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2853" class="Function">ap</a>

          <a id="23601" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23603" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#22762" class="Function">correct-transposition-conjugation-equiv-list</a> <a id="23648" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23321" class="Bound">li</a> <a id="23651" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23325" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23652" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="23655" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1239" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
          <a id="23667" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23669" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2853" class="Function">ap</a>
            <a id="23684" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23686" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="23688" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23688" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="23690" class="Symbol">→</a>
              <a id="23706" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a>
                <a id="23732" class="Symbol">((((</a><a id="23736" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17695" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="23738" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7843" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="23741" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#5959" class="Function">transposition</a> <a id="23755" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17671" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="23757" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23758" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="23762" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23319" class="Bound">t</a><a id="23763" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23765" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23766" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="23770" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23319" class="Bound">t</a><a id="23771" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="23774" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7843" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="23777" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23688" class="Bound">g</a><a id="23778" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23780" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7843" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="23783" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#6121" class="Function">permutation-list-transpositions</a> <a id="23815" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17671" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="23817" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23321" class="Bound">li</a><a id="23819" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23821" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7843" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="23824" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5707" class="Function">inv-equiv</a> <a id="23834" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17695" class="Bound">e</a><a id="23835" class="Symbol">)</a>
                <a id="23853" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23855" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23325" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23856" class="Symbol">))</a>
            <a id="23871" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23873" href="foundation.equivalences.html#16498" class="Function">left-inverse-law-equiv</a> <a id="23896" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#17695" class="Bound">e</a><a id="23897" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
### For all `n : ℕ`, for each transposition of `Fin n`, there exists a matching transposition in `Fin (succ-ℕ n)`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Fin-succ-Fin-transposition"></a><a id="24030" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24030" class="Function">Fin-succ-Fin-transposition</a> <a id="24057" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24059" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24060" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24060" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="24062" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24064" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1444" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="24065" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24067" class="Symbol">→</a> 
  <a id="24072" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24074" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#502" class="Record">Σ</a>

    <a id="24116" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24118" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="24120" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24120" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="24122" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24124" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4379" class="Function">has-cardinality</a> <a id="24140" class="Number">2</a> <a id="24142" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24143" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#502" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24145" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24146" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2072" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="24150" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24060" class="Bound">n</a><a id="24151" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24153" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="24156" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24156" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24158" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24160" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#2131" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="24180" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24181" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24120" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="24183" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24156" class="Bound">x</a><a id="24184" class="Symbol">)))))</a> <a id="24190" class="Symbol">→</a> 
    <a id="24197" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24199" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#502" class="Record">Σ</a>

      <a id="24254" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24256" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="24258" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24258" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="24260" class="Symbol">→</a>
        <a id="24270" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4379" class="Function">has-cardinality</a> <a id="24286" class="Number">2</a>
          <a id="24298" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24300" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#502" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24302" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24303" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2072" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="24307" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24308" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1478" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="24315" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24060" class="Bound">n</a><a id="24316" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24319" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="24322" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24322" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24324" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24326" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#2131" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="24346" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24347" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24258" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="24349" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24322" class="Bound">x</a><a id="24350" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
